coin-or-Couenne-doc in fedora-32

This page displays detail informations of the coin-or-Couenne-doc package. You might want go back to the main page of coin-or-Couenne-doc.

Changelog

Date Author Change
2020-02-21 Jerry James - 0.5.8-1 - Release 0.5.8 - Drop upstreamed -format patch - Make the -doc subpackage be arch-specific to work around FTBFS
2020-01-28 Fedora Release Engineering - 0.5.7-4 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_32_Mass_Rebuild
2019-07-24 Fedora Release Engineering - 0.5.7-3 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_31_Mass_Rebuild
2019-06-27 Jerry James - 0.5.7-2 - Update project URL - Eliminate unnecessary BRs and Rs - Build with nauty support - Add -format patch - Force libtool to not defeat -Wl,--as-needed - Be explicit about library versions as required by latest guidelines - Filter out unnecessary Libs values from pkgconfig files - Package doxygen tag file to enable cross-linking
2019-04-09 Antonio Trande - 0.5.7-1 - Release 0.5.7
2019-01-31 Fedora Release Engineering - 0.5.6-18 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_30_Mass_Rebuild
2018-11-01 Antonio Trande - 0.5.6-17 - Remove Group tags
2018-07-12 Fedora Release Engineering - 0.5.6-16 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_29_Mass_Rebuild

2018-02-23 Antonio Trande - 0.5.6-14 - Rebuild for Ipopt-3.12.9 - Rebuild against openblas
